<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：自身</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：敏捷值</font><font face="宋体">/轮</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：盗贼进入高度戒备状态，更有效的偏移敌人的攻击并降低自身承受的伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你每次受到近战攻击，你在防御上就获得传奇敏捷</font><font face="宋体">/点偏斜加值并且获得1点全伤害抵消和1点全伤害忽略，你获得偏斜防御最大不超过白刃技能等级/点；你获得的全伤害抵消和全伤害忽略效果最大不超过你传奇敏捷/点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若你在一轮内未受到攻击，则</font><font face="宋体">“备战就绪”带来的好处立即结束，但是“备战就绪”会根据原本的持续时间继续存在。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 11.3pt 0pt 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">致命投掷</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：反射动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">5点意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：一次投掷攻击的射程</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：你对准敌人的咽喉，投掷出一把致命的匕首。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：使用致命投掷，你必须扔出一把</font><font face="宋体">“暗器”或者“匕首”，若你没有可以用于投掷的“暗器”和“匕首”，则你无法使用本招式；发动“致命投掷”会自动消耗你全部的“连击点”。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你以反射动作进行一次轻投掷武器攻击检定，若成功命中目标，则不会对目标造成伤害伤害，而是改为你使目标的基础移动速度降低</font><font face="宋体">12米，持续一轮，你使用“致命投掷”时根据消耗的“连击点”数量不同对目标会造成不同的额外效果：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">1点连击点-你对目标造成5点穿刺物理严重伤害；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">2点连击点-你对目标造成10点穿刺物理严重伤害；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">3点连击点-你对目标造成21点穿刺物理严重伤害；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">4点连击点-你对目标造成41点穿刺物理严重伤害；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">5点连击点-在造成41点穿刺物理严重伤害的同时，此次“致命投掷”还会获得额外效果：若被你以“致命投掷”攻击的目标正在施法，你以反射动作进行一次轻投掷武器攻击检定，和目标的此次施法检定进行对抗（若目标那个法术无需检定，则进行一次心灵检定），若你胜出，则你将目标此次的施法动作打断，目标因此消耗的能量和动作并不会返还；并且当你成功打断目标施法时，你使目标在接下来的时间里无法使用该系法术，效果持续一轮。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">例：轮回者钱包正施展法术</font><font face="宋体">“猎者智慧”，且钱包位于轮回者奏鸣雪投掷攻击的射程内，奏鸣雪以轻投掷武器攻击检定与钱包的施法检定进行对抗，若奏鸣雪胜出，则打断钱包的“猎者智慧”法术，并且由于“猎者智慧”法术的专业包括变化和预言，在接下来一轮时间里，钱包无法使用变化系和预言系的法术。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 11.3pt 0pt 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">肾击</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">3点意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：触及</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：盗贼沉重的打击对手，将目标击晕。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：这个终结技需要你有至少</font><font face="宋体">1点“连击点”才可以使用，根据你消耗的“连击点”的数量不同，这个终结技的效果也不同。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">1点连击点-你进行一次近战白刃攻击，这次攻击不造成伤害，而是对目标造成此次近战白刃攻击原本所应该造成伤害值/点晕眩点数，该晕眩点数不可叠加，目标以强韧豁免，承受豁免差值/点；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">2点连击点-你进行一次近战白刃攻击，这次攻击不造成伤害，而是对目标造成此次近战白刃攻击检定成功数/点晕眩点数，该晕眩点数不可叠加，目标以强韧豁免，承受豁免差值/点；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">3点连击点-你进行一次近战白刃攻击检定，这次攻击不造成伤害，而是对目标造成此次近战白刃攻击检定成功数/点晕眩点数，该晕眩点数不可叠加，目标以强韧豁免，承受豁免差值/点；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">4点连击点-你进行一次近战白刃攻击检定，这次攻击不造成伤害，而是对目标造成此次近战白刃攻击检定成功数/点晕眩点数，该晕眩点数可以叠加，可以造成重度不良状态，目标以强韧豁免，但是豁免检定会承受你白刃技能等级/点招式减值，承受豁免差值/点；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">5点连击点-你进行一次近战白刃攻击检定，这次攻击不造成伤害，而是对目标造成此次近战白刃攻击检定成功数/点晕眩点数，该晕眩点数不可豁免，可以叠加，可以造成重度不良状态。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 11.3pt 0pt 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">切割</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">3点意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：这个终结技需要你有至少</font><font face="宋体">1点“连击点”才可以使用，根据你消耗的“连击点”的数量不同，这个终结技的效果也不同。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“切割”技能持续期间，你的攻击速度得到极大提高，这体现为：你可以以移动动作进行一些需要标准动作进行的行动（如进行一次攻击，施展一个动作需求为标准动作的技能等）；你的先攻值增加白刃技能等级/点，这会影响先攻顺序。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：每场战斗开始时，你可以宣言一种不良状态点数（如恐惧点数、晕眩点数、精神束缚点数、纠缠点数等），一经选定不可更改。随后在本场战斗中，你对身上存在该种不良状态点数的目标进行近战白刃攻击时，攻击检定会获得</font><font face="宋体">X点招式加值，X等于目标当前承受的该种不良状态点数的数值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本招式加值的上限为你的（敏捷值</font><font face="宋体">+白刃技能等级）/点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：盗贼使自己快速潜入阴影位面，在现实与阴影的夹缝之间，寻常的手段根本无法辨认出盗贼所在的位置。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你可以选择立刻移除自身当前正承受的</font><font face="宋体">4项会影响自身移动的不良状态点数和不良状态；同时，你立即进入隐身状态，这是一个A级的魔幻本质反侦测能力，并且在持续时间内你无法被精确定位。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：（传奇敏捷</font><font face="宋体">+1）/轮</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：盗贼用阴影的力量包裹自己的身体，使自己免疫法术的力量。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你立即移除自身所承受的所有由法术带来的不良状态点数和不良状态；并且在</font><font face="宋体">“暗影斗篷”持续时间里，你免疫S级以下级别法术对你带来的效果（包括伤害），但不影响不针对自己的效果（如施法者自身），或针对环境的效果（目标可以正常施展范围法术，但是你自己会免疫那个范围法术），同时你还能够使目标拥有的能够影响到你的相关效果无效化，但不会限制对手对自身或环境的效果（如范围法术）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">某些特定的情况下，某些法术造成的效果可能会使你丧失动作（如时间停止），这种情况下，只要你在施展本能力后可以恢复行动，那么你就可以发动本能力，按照你如常拥有该动作计算。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：只有最高深的盗贼才能掌握的特殊技巧，将自己与阴影同化，快速从他人背后的影子里钻出，在敌人来不及反应间将敌人杀死。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你立即传送到自身模糊感知范围内任意一个目标的背后</font><font face="宋体">——暗影步；在成功进行一次传送后，你的基础移动速度增加敏捷值/米，持续一轮（在一轮内多次使用暗影步不会使基础移动速度再次增加）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个</font><font face="宋体">A级别的空间效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">摄入方式：本毒素只能通过伤口进入。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">中毒：目标施展法术时，所需要的动作提升一级（迅捷动作</font><font face="宋体">/反射动作-移动动作-标准动作-整轮动作，最多提升为整轮动作）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是</font><font face="宋体">D级毒素效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 11.3pt 0pt 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
